		particleType		= PT_3D_PLANE
		Emitrate			= 5
		Lifetime			= 1.500
		NumParticles		= 10
		TriggerTime			= 1000000000
		Layer				= 14
		Emitradius			= XYZ(0, 300, 0)
		BillBoardType		= BT_NONE
		SourceBlendMode	= D3DBLEND_SRCALPHA
		DestBlendMode	= D3DBLEND_INVSRCALPHA
		Trace				= TRUE

		Initial						Texture = "water_fall_Wave.tga"
		Initial						Color = RGBA(0, 0, 1, 0)
		Fade so From 0.010 to 0.500	Color = RGBA(1, 1, 1, 1)
		Fade so From 0.800 to 1.500	Color = RGBA(0, 1, 0, 0)
		Initial						Size = XYZ(1000, 1000, 1)
		Fade so From 0.000 to 1.500	Size = XYZ(300, 300, 1)
		Initial						Scale = 1.500
		Initial						Rotate = XYZ(0, -45, random(-10, 10))
		Fade so From 0.000 to 1.500	Rotate = XYZ(0, -45, random(-10, 10))
	}
